<!-- 统一注册登录 begin -->
<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[
function chkLogin(){
	var username = document.showLogin.username.value;
	var password = document.showLogin.password.value;
	var loginType = document.showLogin.entry.value;
	if(username.length < 1 || username.length > 64){
		alert("用户名非法，请检查!");
		return false;
	}
	if(password.length < 1 || password.length > 30){
		alert("密码非法，请检查!");
		return false;
	}
	if(loginType == "null"){
		alert("您还没有选择要登录到哪里，请您选择去向！");
		sina.$("loginFldselectop").style.display = "block";
		sina.addEvent(document.body,"mousedown",LoginSelectClickOther);
		return false;
	}
	if(loginType == "263mail"){  //263.sina.com只接受帐号@之前的部分
		var p = username.indexOf("@");
		var u = p == -1 ? username : username.substr(0, p);
		document.form_04.u.value = u;
		document.form_04.psw.value = password;
		document.form_04.submit();
		//document.showLogin.password.value = "";
		setTimeout('document.showLogin.password.value = ""',500);
		return false;
	}
	if(username.indexOf("@") == -1 && loginType == "vipmail"){
		document.showLogin.username.value += "@vip.sina.com";
	}
	document.showLogin.submit();
	//document.showLogin.password.value = "";
	setTimeout('document.showLogin.password.value = ""',500);
	return false;
}
function chkLoginType(username){
	username = username.toLowerCase();
	if(username.indexOf("@") != -1){
		sina.$("L_freemail").className = "disabled";
		sina.$("L_freemail").onclick = null;
		sina.$("L_vipmail").className = "disabled";
		sina.$("L_vipmail").onclick = null;
		sina.$("L_2008mail").className = "disabled";
		sina.$("L_2008mail").onclick = null;
		sina.$("L_263mail").className = "disabled";
		sina.$("L_263mail").onclick = null;
		sina.$("L_cnmail").className = "disabled";
		sina.$("L_cnmail").onclick = null;
	}else{
		sina.$("L_freemail").className = "";
		sina.$("L_freemail").onclick = function(){LoginSelect("freemail")};
		sina.$("L_vipmail").className = "";
		sina.$("L_vipmail").onclick = function(){LoginSelect("vipmail")};
		sina.$("L_2008mail").className = "";
		sina.$("L_2008mail").onclick = function(){LoginSelect("2008mail")};
		sina.$("L_263mail").className = "";
		sina.$("L_263mail").onclick = function(){LoginSelect("263mail")};
		sina.$("L_cnmail").className = "";
		sina.$("L_cnmail").onclick = function(){LoginSelect("cnmail")};
		return;
	};
	if(username.indexOf("@sina.com") != -1){
		sina.$("L_freemail").className = "";
		sina.$("L_freemail").onclick = function(){LoginSelect("freemail")};
		LoginSelect("freemail");
	};
	if(username.indexOf("@vip.sina.com") != -1){
		sina.$("L_vipmail").className = "";
		sina.$("L_vipmail").onclick = function(){LoginSelect("vipmail")};
		LoginSelect("vipmail");
	};
	if(username.indexOf("@2008.sina.com") != -1){
		sina.$("L_2008mail").className = "";
		sina.$("L_2008mail").onclick = function(){LoginSelect("2008mail")};
		LoginSelect("2008mail");
	};
	if(username.indexOf("@263.sina.com") != -1){
		sina.$("L_263mail").className = "";
		sina.$("L_263mail").onclick = function(){LoginSelect("263mail")};
		LoginSelect("263mail");
	};
	if(username.indexOf("@sina.cn") != -1){
		sina.$("L_cnmail").className = "";
		sina.$("L_cnmail").onclick = function(){LoginSelect("cnmail")};
		LoginSelect("cnmail");
	};
};
var sina = {
	$ : function(objName){if(document.getElementById){return eval('document.getElementById("'+objName+'")')}else{return eval('document.all.'+objName)}},
	isIE : navigator.appVersion.indexOf("MSIE")!=-1?true:false,
	addEvent : function(obj,eventType,func){if(obj.attachEvent){obj.attachEvent("on" + eventType,func);}else{obj.addEventListener(eventType,func,false)}},
	delEvent : function(obj,eventType,func){
		if(obj.detachEvent){obj.detachEvent("on" + eventType,func)}else{obj.removeEventListener(eventType,func,false)}
	},
	readCookie : function(l){var i="",I=l+"=";if(document.cookie.length>0){offset=document.cookie.indexOf(I);if(offset!=-1){offset+=I.length;end=document.cookie.indexOf(";",offset);if(end==-1)end=document.cookie.length;i=unescape(document.cookie.substring(offset,end))}};return i},
	writeCookie : function(O,o,l,I){var i="",c="";if(l!=null){i=new Date((new Date).getTime()+l*3600000);i="; expires="+i.toGMTString()};if(I!=null){c=";domain="+I};document.cookie=O+"="+escape(o)+i+c}
};
function LoginSelectClickOther(e){
	thisObj = e.target?e.target:event.srcElement;
	do{
		if(thisObj.id == "loginFldselect" || thisObj == document.showLogin.password) return;
		if(thisObj.tagName == "BODY"){LoginSelectClose();return;};
		thisObj = thisObj.parentNode;
	}while(thisObj.parentNode);
};
function clickLoginSelect(){
	if(sina.$("loginFldselectop").style.display == "block"){
		LoginSelectClose();
	}else{
		sina.$("loginFldselectop").style.display = "block";
		sina.addEvent(document.body,"mousedown",LoginSelectClickOther);
	}
};
function LoginSelectClose(){
	sina.$("loginFldselectop").style.display = "none";
	sina.delEvent(document.body,"mousedown",LoginSelectClickOther);
};
function LoginSelect(title){
	var titleName;
	switch(title){
		case "cnmail":
			document.showLogin.entry.value = "cnmail";
			titleName = "CN邮箱";
			break;
		case "freemail":
			document.showLogin.entry.value = "freemail";
			titleName = "免费邮箱";
			break;
		case "vipmail":
			document.showLogin.entry.value = "vipmail";
			titleName = "VIP邮箱";
			break;
		case "2008mail":
			document.showLogin.entry.value = "2008mail";
			titleName = "2008邮箱";
			break;
		case "263mail":
			document.showLogin.entry.value = "263mail";
			titleName = "同名邮箱";
			break;
		case "blog":
			document.showLogin.entry.value = "blog";
			titleName = "博客";
			break;
		case "vblog":
			document.showLogin.entry.value = "vblog";
			titleName = "播客";
			break;	
		case "miniblog":
			document.showLogin.entry.value = "miniblog";
			titleName = "微博";
			break;
		case "bar":
			document.showLogin.entry.value = "tieba";
			titleName = "贴吧";
			break;
		case "bbs":
			document.showLogin.entry.value = "forum";
			titleName = "论坛";
			break;
		case "login":
			document.showLogin.entry.value = "sso";
			titleName = "会员中心";
			break;
	};
	sina.$("loginFldselectdis").innerHTML = titleName;
	sina.writeCookie("loginType",title,2160,"sina.com.cn;path=/");
	if(document.showLogin.username.value != "" && document.showLogin.password.value != ""){
		document.showLogin.onsubmit();
	};
	LoginSelectClose();
};
function openLoginType(){
	if(document.showLogin.username.value != "" && document.showLogin.username.value.indexOf("@") == -1 && sina.$("loginFldselectdis").innerHTML == "选择去向"){
		sina.$("loginFldselectop").style.display = "block";
		sina.addEvent(document.body,"mousedown",LoginSelectClickOther);
	}
}

				fn.action="http://q.blog.sina.com.cn/group_search.php";
			} else {
				if(document.forms["iask_f"].t.selectedIndex==2){
					document.getElementById("s").value=0;
					fn.action="http://search.blog.sina.com.cn/blog/search";
				} else {
					fn.action="http://search.blog.sina.com.cn/blog/search";
				}				//fn.action="http://search.blog.sina.com.cn/blog/search";
			}
		} else {
			return false;
		}
        fn.submit();
        return false;
}

	try{
		new Image().src = "http://mark.sina.com.cn/v2/hot_pv.php?keyword="+keyword+"&hwfrom="+hwfrom+"&tag="+tag+"&_d="+(new Date()).getTime()+"&url="+a.href;
	}catch(ex){
	}
	return true;
}

		new Image().src = "http://mark.sina.com.cn/v2/blog_hot_pv.php?keyword="+a.innerHTML+"&hwfrom="+hwfrom+"&tag=4&_d="+(new Date()).getTime()+"&url="+a.href;
	}catch(ex){
	}
	return true;
}

	try{
		if (typeof(keyword) == "undefined")

			keyword = a.innerHTML;
		}
		new Image().src = "http://mark.sina.com.cn/v2/hot_pv.php?keyword="+keyword+"&hwfrom="+hwfrom+"&tag=5&_d="+(new Date()).getTime()+"&url="+a.href;
	}catch(ex){
	}
	return true;
}

	}catch(ex){
	}
	return true;
}
function SetHome(obj){
	try{
		obj.style.behavior='url(#default#homepage)';
		obj.setHomePage('http://www.sina.com.cn/');
	}catch(e){
		if(window.netscape){
			try{
				netscape.security.PrivilegeManager.enablePrivilege("UniversalXPConnect");
			}catch(e){
				alert("抱歉，此操作被浏览器拒绝！\n\n请在浏览器地址栏输入“about:config”并回车然后将[signed.applets.codebase_principal_support]设置为'true'");
			};
		}else{
			alert("抱歉，您所使用的浏览器无法完成此操作。\n\n您需要手动将'http://www.sina.com.cn/'设置为首页。");
		};
	};
};

var o = new SinaDotAdJs();
var hsnum = 3;
function houselink9(id){
	for(var i=1;i<=hsnum;i++){
	o.$("HSBtn"+i).className = "out01";
	if(i==2){o.$("HSBtn"+i).className = "out02";}
	o.$("HSCon"+i).className = "houseSearchC hide";
	}
	o.$("HSBtn"+id).className = "act01";
	if(id==2){o.$("HSBtn"+id).className = "act02";}
	o.$("HSCon"+id).className = "houseSearchC";
}
function clearInputValue(t)
{
	if (t.value == '' || t.value != '请输入楼盘名称')
	{
		t.value = '';
	}
}
function LejuMenu_setTab(a,b){
  for(var i=1;i<=b;i++){
    var menu=document.getElementById('sina_leju_menu_t'+i);
    var con=document.getElementById('sina_leju_menu_c'+i);
    menu.className=i==a?"on":"";
    con.style.display=i==a?"block":"none";
  } 
}

		function submitFormWithChannel(channelname){
			if(document.gform.q.value=="请输入关键词"||document.gform.q.value==""){
				document.gform.q.value="";
				document.gform.channel.value=channelname;
				document.gform.submit();
			}else{
				document.gform.channel.value=channelname;
				new Image().src="http://js.iask.com/cW.png?type=GOOGLE&k="+ document.gform.q.value +"&idx=2";
				document.gform.submit();
				return;
			}
		}
		function checkGoogleValue(){
			if(document.gform.q.value=="请输入关键词"||document.gform.q.value==""){
				document.gform.q.value="";
			}
			document.gform.channel.value = "hpsearch";
			new Image().src="http://js.iask.com/cW.png?type=GOOGLE&k="+ document.gform.q.value +"&idx=1";
			return true;
		}
		/* google end */

{
	window.open("http://ditu.iask.com/#type=0&pars=0010,"+document.getElementById('key').value+",,,,,,,");
	return false;
}
		/* ditu end */
		/* shishiren begin */
		function iask_ck(){
			if(document.f.key.value == ""){
				window.open("http://iask.sina.com.cn/");
			}
			return true;
		}
		function ask(){
			if(document.f.key.value == ""){
				window.open("http://iask.sina.com.cn/");
				return false;
			}else{
				window.open("http://iask.sina.com.cn/question/ask_new_2.php?title=" + document.f.key.value);
				return false;
			}
		}
		/* zhishiren end */
		/* ishare begin */
		function checkishare(){
			if(document.f.key.value == ""){
				window.open("http://ishare.iask.sina.com.cn/");
				return false;
			}else{
				return;
			}
		}
		/* ishare end */

function strToDate(str,ext){
	if(str==null || str=='') return;
	var arys = new Array();
	arys = str.split('-');
	var newDate = new Date(arys[0],arys[1]-1,arys[2],9,0,0);
	if(ext){
		newDate = new Date(newDate.getTime()+1000*60*60*24);
	}
	return newDate;
}

<script>
function trim(str)
{  
	return str.replace(/(^\s*)|(\s*$)/g, "").replace(/(^　*)|(　*$)/g, "");
}
function goLife()
{
	var temp=document.getElementsByName("lifecity");  
	var cityname = '';
	for (i=0;i<temp.length;i++){  
		  if(temp[i].checked){
		   	city = temp[i].id;
		   	cityname = temp[i].value;
		  } 
	}
	what = document.getElementsByName("keyword")[0].value;
	what = trim(what);
	if(what=="查餐馆休闲健身"){
		what='';
	}
	return lifesearchLocation(city,what,cityname);
}
function lifesearchLocation(city,what,cityname)
{
	life_site_host = 'life.sina.com.cn';
	if(!city)	city=2;
	var uwhat	= what;
	var url = _uwhat ='';
	if(uwhat)	{
		uwhat = encodeURIComponent(encodeURIComponent(uwhat));
		_uwhat = '--utf-1--all-1--?what-'+uwhat;
	var url  ='http://' + life_site_host + '/search/city-'+city+'--class-0'+_uwhat;
	}else
	{
		var url  ='http://' + life_site_host+'/'+cityname;
	}
	window.open(url,"_blank");   
	return false;
}

            (function(){
                NTES.ui.PopUpLayer = function(ctrl, content){
                    var timerId;
                    function show(){
                        content.style.display = "block";
                    }
                    function hide(){
                        content.style.display = "none";
                    }
                    function delayHide(){
                        clearTimer();
                        timerId = setTimeout(hide, 300);
                    }
                    function clearTimer(){
                        if (timerId) {
                            clearTimeout(timerId);
                            timerId = null;
                        }
                    }
                    NTES.event.addEvent(ctrl, "click", show);
                    NTES.event.addEvent(ctrl, "mouseout", delayHide);
                    NTES.event.addEvent(ctrl, "mouseover", clearTimer);
                    NTES.event.addEvent(content, "mouseover", clearTimer);
                    NTES.event.addEvent(content, "mouseout", delayHide);
                };
                var dayCountInMonths = [31, 28, 31, 30, 31, 30, 31, 31, 30, 31, 30, 31];
                NTES.ui.Calendar = function(year, month){
                    this.constructor = arguments.callee;
                    this.setDate(year, month);
                };
                NTES.ui.Calendar.prototype = {
                    getYear: function(){
                        return this._year;
                    },
                    getMonth: function(){
                        return this._month + 1;
                    },
                    setDate: function(y, m){
                        var now = new Date();
                        this._year = isNaN(y) ? now.getFullYear() : y;
                        this._month = isNaN(m) ? now.getMonth() : m - 1;
                    },
                    draw: function(tpl){
                        var dayCount = NTES.ui.Calendar.getDayCount(this._year, this._month + 1), tool = new Date(this._year, this._month, 1), now = new Date(), firstDay = tool.getDay(), data = {
                            year: this._year,
                            month: this._month + 1,
                            weeks: []
                        }, i, state, temp, week = [];
                        now.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
                        now = now.getTime();
                        while (firstDay-- > 0) {
                            week.push({
                                value: ""
                            });
                        }
                        for (i = 1; i <= dayCount; i++) {
                            tool.setDate(i);
                            temp = tool.getTime();
                            if (temp > now) {
                                state = -1;
                            }
                            else 
                                if (temp < now) {
                                    state = 1;
                                }
                                else {
                                    state = 0;
                                }
                            week.push({
                                value: i,
                                state: state
                            });
                            if (week.length === 7) {
                                data.weeks.push(week);
                                week = [];
                            }
                        }
                        if (week.length % 7 !== 0) { // 补全后面的空白
                            while (week.length < 7) {
                                week.push({
                                    value: ""
                                });
                            }
                            data.weeks.push(week);
                        }
                        return NTES.util.parseTpl(tpl, data);
                    }
                };
                NTES.ui.Calendar.getDayCount = function(y, m){
                    return 2 == m ? (0 == y % 4 && 0 != y % 100 || 0 == y % 400 ? 29 : 28) : dayCountInMonths[m - 1];
                };
            })();

var houseIPQuery=new Object();
(function() {
var china = {
	north : "|北京市|天津市|河北省|山西省|内蒙古|辽宁省|吉林省|黑龙江省|山东省|",
	east : "|上海市|江苏省|浙江省|安徽省|江西省|",
        sichuan : "|四川省|",
	shenzhen : "|深圳市|",
	south : "|广东省|",
	others : "|广州市|"
};
var locQuery = {
	url : "http://ip.ws.126.net/ipquery",
	cookieName : "locOfCh",
	exec : function(onComplete) {
		var result = NTES.cookie.get(this.cookieName);
		if (result != "" && china.hasOwnProperty(result)) {
			onComplete(result);
		} else {
			NTES.ajax.importJs(this.url, function() {
				if (typeof lo != "undefined" && typeof lc != "undefined") {
					var tempO = "|" + lo + "|", tempC = "|" + lc + "|";
					if (china.north.indexOf(tempO) != -1) {
						result = "north";
					} else if (china.east.indexOf(tempO) != -1) {
						result = "east";
					} else if (china.shenzhen.indexOf(tempC) != -1) {
						result = "shenzhen";
					} else if (china.sichuan.indexOf(tempO) != -1) {
						result = "sichuan";
					}else if (china.south.indexOf(tempO) != -1) {
						result = "south";
					} else {
						result = "others";
					}
				}
				if (result) {
					NTES.cookie.set(locQuery.cookieName, result, '1M',".163.com");
					onComplete(result);
				}
			});
		}
	}
};
houseIPQuery = locQuery;
})();            houseIPQuery.exec(function(loc){
                //north:北京 east:上海 shenzhen:深圳 others:广州
                if (loc == "north") {
                    $("#house_bj").style.display = "block";
					$("#newhouse_bj").style.display ="block";
                    $("#house_gz").style.display = "none";
					$("#newhouse_gz").style.display ="none";
                }
                else 
                    if (loc == "east") {
                        $("#house_sh").style.display = "block";
						$("#newhouse_sh").style.display ="block";
                        $("#house_gz").style.display = "none";
						$("#newhouse_gz").style.display ="none";
                    }
                    else 
                        if (loc == "shenzhen") {
                            $("#house_sz").style.display = "block";
							$("#newhouse_sz").style.display ="block";
                            $("#house_gz").style.display = "none";
							$("#newhouse_gz").style.display ="none";
                        }
            });

function AddFavorite(sURL, sTitle){
	try{
		window.external.addFavorite(sURL, sTitle);
	}
	catch (e){
		try{
			window.sidebar.addPanel(sTitle, sURL, "");
		}catch (e){
			alert("加入收藏失败，请使用Ctrl+D进行添加");
		}
	}
}
function SetHome(obj,vrl){
	try{
		obj.style.behavior='url(#default#homepage)';
		obj.setHomePage(vrl);
	}catch(e){
		if(window.netscape){
			try{
				netscape.security.PrivilegeManager.enablePrivilege("UniversalXPConnect");
			}catch(e){
				alert("抱歉，此操作被浏览器拒绝！\n\n请在浏览器地址栏输入“about:config”并回车然后将[signed.applets.codebase_principal_support]设置为'true'");
			}
		}else{
			alert("抱歉，您所使用的浏览器无法完成此操作。\n\n您需要手动将'http://money.163.com/stock/'设置为首页。");
		}
	}
}
var stockSuggest2 = new ntesStockSuggest({
	// 输入框id
	inputid: "socode2",
	// 记录数
	max: 10,
	tooltip: "代码/拼音/名称",
	// 左对齐的元素, 没有则按输入框
	posElem: "selstockinput2",
	// 获取查询类型HS/HK/US/...
	getType: function(){
		var sel = document.getElementById("selstockinput2");
		return sel.options[sel.selectedIndex].value;
	},
	// 选中某一项
	callback: function(item){
		typeMap = {
			"SH":"http://quotes.money.163.com/0{0}.html",
			"SZ":"http://quotes.money.163.com/1{0}.html",
			"HK":"http://hkquotes.money.163.com/html/{0}.html",
			"FX":"http://quotes.money.163.com/forex/hq/{0}.html",
			"US":"http://quotes.money.163.com/usstock/hq/{0}.html",
			"FN":"http://quotes.fund.163.com/html/{0}.html",
			"FU":"http://quotes.money.163.com/futures/hq/{0}.html"
		};
		url = typeMap[item["type"]].replace("{0}",  item["symbol"]);
		window.open(url);
	}
});

		alert("请选择要查看的股票");

             function PopUpLayer(ctrl, content) {
				var timerId;
				var hide = function() {
					content.style.display = "none";
				};
				this.hide = function(event) {
					timerId = setTimeout(hide, 300);
				};
				ctrl.addEvent("mouseover", function() { content.style.display = "block"; });
				ctrl.addEvent("mouseout", this.hide);
				content.addEvent("mouseout", this.hide);
				content.addEvent("mouseover", function() { clearTimeout(timerId); });
			}
 			var calendarLayer = new PopUpLayer(NTES("#getCalendar"), NTES("#calendarBox"));
            //日历Start
            function calendar(year, month){
                //Get current Date
                var cDate = new Date();
                var cYear = cDate.getFullYear();
                var cMonth = cDate.getMonth();
                var cDay = cDate.getDate();
                var yearDom = NTES("#setYear");
                var monthDom = NTES("#setMonth");
                if (arguments.length > 1) {
                    this.year = year;
                    this.month = month - 1;
                }
                else {
                    this.year = cYear;
                    this.month = cMonth;
                    //显示日期
                    yearDom.innerHTML = cYear;
                    monthDom.innerHTML = cMonth + 1;
                }
                this.date = cDay;
                this.draw(printCalendar);
            }
            //获的月的天数
            calendar.prototype.monthDayNum = function(year, month){
                var tdate = new Date(year, month + 1, 0);
                return tdate.getDate();
            }
            //获的指定1号是星期几
            calendar.prototype.dayInWeek = function(year, month, date){
                var tdate = new Date(year, month, date);
                return tdate.getDay();
            }
            //打印日历
            calendar.prototype.draw = function(callback){
                var year = this.year;
                var month = this.month;
                var currentDay = this.date;
                var firstDayInWeek = this.dayInWeek(year, month, 1);
                var monthDayNum = this.monthDayNum(year, month, 0);
                callback(year, month, currentDay, firstDayInWeek, monthDayNum);
            }
            //上一月 下一月
            function calendarNP(yearID, monthID, state){
                var yearDom = NTES(yearID);
                var monthDom = NTES(monthID);
                var year = parseInt(yearDom.innerHTML);
                var month = parseInt(monthDom.innerHTML);
                if (state == "next") {
                    month = month + 1;
                    if (month > 12) {
                        month = 1;
                        year = year + 1;
                    }
                }
                if (state == "previous") {
                    month = month - 1;
                    if (month == 0) {
                        month = 12;
                        year = year - 1;
                    }
                }
                yearDom.innerHTML = year;
                monthDom.innerHTML = month;
                var tcalendar = new calendar(year, month);
            }
            //显示日历
            function printCalendar(year, month, currentDay, firstDayInWeek, monthDayNum){
                var year = year;
                var month = month;
                var currentDay = currentDay;
                var firstDayInWeek = firstDayInWeek;
                var monthDayNum = monthDayNum;
                var displayMonth, displayDay;
                var calendarList = NTES("#calendarList");
                var liarray = [];
                if (month < 9) {
                    month = month + 1
                    displayMonth = "0" + month;
                }
                else {
                    displayMonth = month + 1;
                }
                for (var i = 0; i < firstDayInWeek; i++) {
                    liarray.push("<li></li>");
                }
                for (var j = 1; j <= monthDayNum; j++) {
                    if (j < 10) {
                        displayDay = "0" + j;
                    }
                    else {
                        displayDay = j;
                    }
                    if (j == currentDay) {
                        liarray.push("<li><a class=\"current\" href=\"http://post2.news.163.com/wgethtml/http+!!money.163.com!stock!/" + year + "-" + displayMonth + "/" + displayDay + "/12.html\">" + j + "</a></li>");
                    }
                    else {
                        liarray.push("<li><a href=\"http://post2.news.163.com/wgethtml/http+!!money.163.com!stock!/" + year + "-" + displayMonth + "/" + displayDay + "/12.html\">" + j + "</a></li>");
                    }
                }
                var str = liarray.join("");
                calendarList.innerHTML = str;
            }

ntesQuote.addFormatHandler("trendbg", function(code, meta, elem, quoteData){
	if(!quoteData) return;
	var preQuote = ntesQuote.getPreQuote(code);
	if(!preQuote) return;
	var attr = meta["_trendby"];
	if(!attr) return;
	var data = quoteData[attr];
	if(!data) return;
	var preData = preQuote[attr];
	if(!preData) return;
	elem.className = data>preData ? "upbg" : (data<preData ? "downbg" : "　");
	var timeout = (meta["timeout"] || 1500)*1;
	window.setTimeout(function(){
		elem.className = "";
	}, timeout);
});

					if (date !="Min"){

					}else{
						NTES("#pzpic").src =pzhref+"COSH&Height=100&Width=160&DataType=Min";
					}
				}else {
					if (date !="Min"){
						NTES("#pzpic").src =pzhref+pz+"&Height=100&Width=160&DataType=Day&DataArea="+date;
					}else{
						NTES("#pzpic").src =pzhref+pz+"&Height=100&Width=160&DataType=Min";
					}
				}
				NTES("#pzname").innerHTML = getpzName(pz);
			}
			//载入世界指数
marketdata.loadGlobalIndex(function(json){
	//名称表
	var names = {"szzs":"上证指数", "hszs":"恒生指数", "dqs":"道琼斯", "nsdk":"纳斯达克", "rmbhl":"人民币汇率", "myzs":"美元指数", "gjyj":"国际油价", "yg":"英国富时", "fg":"法国CAC40", "dg":"德国DAX", "rj":"日经225", "els":"俄罗斯IRTS", "twzs":"台湾指数", "myrmb":"美元/人民币", "hj":"黄金", "blt":"布兰特原油", "ydgs":"印度股市", "bxgs":"巴西股市"};
					for(var name in names){
					var elem = document.getElementById("globalindex_" + name);
					if(!elem) continue;
					//获取该指数数据
					var data = json[name];
					if(!data) continue;
					elem.className = cssColor(percentToNumber(data["ratio"]));
					elem.innerHTML = data["price"] + " (" + data["ratio"] + ")";
				}
	// 要在table里显示的条目
	var items = ["dqs", "nsdk", "hszs", "twzs", "rj", "yg", "fg", "dg", "els", "ydgs", "bxgs"];
	var rows = document.getElementById("globalindextable").getElementsByTagName("tr");
	for(var i=1; i<rows.length && i<items.length+1; i++){
		var code = items[i-1];
		var data = json[code];
		if(!data) continue;
		rows[i].cells[0].innerHTML = names[code];
		rows[i].cells[1].innerHTML = data["price"];
		rows[i].cells[1].className = cssColor(percentToNumber(json[code]["ratio"]));
		rows[i].cells[2].innerHTML = data["ratio"];
		rows[i].cells[2].className = rows[i].cells[1].className;
	}
});

			marketdata.loadCurrencyExchange(function(data){
				// 列表里要显示的名称
				var names = { "美元指数":1, "欧元/美元":1, "英镑/美元":1, "美元/日元":1, "美元/瑞郎":1, "澳币/美元":1, "美元/加币":1, "美元/俄卢布":1, "美元/人民币":1 };
				var trList = document.getElementById("exchangetable").getElementsByTagName("tr");
				var index = 1;
				for(var i=0; i<data.length; i++){
					if(index>=trList.length) break;
					if(names[data[i]["name"]]==1){
						var row = trList[index];
						row.cells[0].innerHTML = formatString("<span title='{0}'>{0}</span>", data[i]["name"]);
						row.cells[1].innerHTML = data[i]["rate"].toFixed(3);
						row.cells[2].innerHTML = data[i]["percent"];
						row.cells[2].className = cssColor(data[i]["updown"]);
						index++;
					}
				}
			});
			//刷新最近访问股的函数 codes格式如：["0600183","0600189"]
			function refreshStockHistory(tableId, codes){
				var rows = document.getElementById(tableId).getElementsByTagName("tr");
				codes[codes.length] = "以下为热门个股";
				var len = codes.length;
				for(var i=len; i<8; i++){
					codes[i] = stockHistory.hot[i-len];
				}
				for(var i=0; i<rows.length-1 && i<codes.length; i++){
					var code = codes[i];
					var row = rows[i+1];
					if(code=="以下为热门个股"){
						var num = row.cells.length;
						for(var a=0; a<num-1; a++){
							row.deleteCell(0);
						}
						row.cells[0].innerHTML = "以下为热门个股";
						row.cells[0].setAttribute("colSpan", 3);
					}else{
						var num = row.cells.length;
						for(var b=num; b<3; b++){
							row.insertCell(0);
						}
						row.cells[0].setAttribute("colSpan", "");
						row.cells[0].innerHTML = formatString("<a href='http://quotes.money.163.com/{0}.html' _quote_='name' code='{0}'>&nbsp;</a>", code);
						row.cells[1].innerHTML = formatString("<span _quote_='arrow' code='{0}'>&nbsp;</span><span _quote_='price' code='{0}'>&nbsp;</span>", code);
						row.cells[2].innerHTML = formatString("<span _quote_='percent' code='{0}'>&nbsp;</span>", code);
					}
				}
				//等待最近访问股载入后刷新报价
				ready(function(){
					//“暂”通过判断jQuote.timeout有没初始化判断是否已经init
					if(typeof(jQuote.timeout)=='undefined'){			
						jQuote.init();
					}
					//部分刷新并载入一次数据
					jQuote.refresh(document.getElementById(tableId)).loadOnce();
				});
			}
			//获取最近访问股代理，刷新列表
			refreshStockHistory("historystock", stockHistory.getCodes());
			//载入自选股 codes为代码数组
			marketdata.loadCustomStock(function(codes){
				var trList = document.getElementById("mystocktable").getElementsByTagName("tr");
				var rows = [];
				for(var i=1; i<trList.length; i++){
					rows.push(trList[i]);
				}
				for(var i=0; i<rows.length && i<codes.length; i++){
					rows[i].cells[0].innerHTML = formatString("<a _quote_='name' code='{0}' target='_blank' href='http://quotes.money.163.com/{0}.html'>{0}</a>", codes[i]);
					rows[i].cells[1].innerHTML = formatString("<span _quote_='price' code='{0}'></span>", codes[i]);
					rows[i].cells[2].innerHTML = formatString("<span _quote_='percent' code='{0}'></span>", codes[i]);
				}
				//设置标记
				window.customStockLoaded = true;
				//等待自选股载入后添加新报价代码
				ready(function(){
					//“暂”通过判断jQuote.timeout有没初始化判断是否已经init
					if(typeof(jQuote.timeout)=='undefined'){			
						jQuote.init();
					}
					//部分刷新并载入一次数据
					jQuote.refresh(document.getElementById("mystocktable")).loadOnce();
				});
			});
			//载入自选强势基金 ,betterFunds为强势基金集合，customFunds为自选的基金代码
			marketdata.fund.loadCustomBetterFunds(function(betterFunds, customFunds){
				if(!customFunds){
					//Cookie里没有自选基金
					var rows = document.getElementById("mybetterfundtable").getElementsByTagName("tr");
					var row = rows[1];
					var num = row.cells.length;
					for(var a=0; a<num-1; a++){
						row.deleteCell(0);
					}
					row.cells[0].innerHTML = "<a target='_blank' href='http://quotes.fund.163.com/fund.html' >您尚未自定义，点击设置关注基金</a>";
					row.cells[0].setAttribute("colSpan", 3);
				}else{
					//缩短名称
					function shortName(name, max){
						return (name && name.length>max) ? name.substring(0, max) : name;
					}
					//将customFunds由[]转成{}
					var fundMap = {};
					for(var i=0; i<customFunds.length; i++){
						fundMap[customFunds[i]] = true;
					}
					var rows = document.getElementById("mybetterfundtable").getElementsByTagName("tr");
					var index=0;
					for(var i=0; i<betterFunds.length && index<rows.length-1; i++){
						var item = betterFunds[i];
						if(!fundMap[item["FundCode"]]) continue; //跳过不是自选的
						var row = rows[index+1];
						index++;
						row.cells[0].innerHTML = formatString("<a target='_blank' href='http://quotes.fund.163.com/fundDetail.html?code={0}' title='{1}'>{2}</a>", item["FundCode"], item["FundName"], shortName(item["FundName"],6));
						row.cells[1].innerHTML = item["UnitNV"];
						row.cells[2].innerHTML = item["GrowthRate"];
						row.cells[2].className = cssColor(percentToNumber(item["GrowthRate"]));
					}
				}
			});

				var rows = document.getElementById("conceptList").getElementsByTagName("tr");

					var row = rows[i+1];
					var item = data[i];
					row.cells[0].innerHTML = item["name"];
					row.cells[1].innerHTML = item["code"];
					row.cells[2].innerHTML = item["price"];
					//因为updown_rate的格式为-0.07 (2.89%)，所以要拆分出涨跌幅
					var ud = item["updown_rate"].substring(0,1)=="-" ? "-" : ""; //正负的符号
					var udrate = ud + item["updown_rate"].substring(item["updown_rate"].indexOf("(")+1,item["updown_rate"].indexOf(")"));
					row.cells[3].innerHTML = udrate;
				}
			});

			//载入A/H股溢价表
			marketdata.loadAHPrice(function(json){
				//按 溢价率降序(A股低于H股的 靠上) 排列
				json.sort(function(obj1, obj2){
					try{
						if(isNaN(obj1["yield"]*1)) return 1;
						if(isNaN(obj2["yield"]*1)) return -1;
						return (obj1["yield"] - obj2["yield"])*(-1);
					}catch(ex){
						return 0;
					}
				});
				var rows = document.getElementById("ah_price_table").getElementsByTagName("tr");
				for(var i=0; i<json.length && i<rows.length-1; i++){
					var row = rows[i+1];
					var item = json[i];
					row.cells[0].innerHTML = formatString("<a href='http://hkquotes.money.163.com/html/{0}.html' target='_blank'>{1}</a>", item["symbol"], item["desp"].substring(0,4));
					row.cells[1].innerHTML = (item["a_price"]*1).toFixed(2);
					row.cells[2].innerHTML = (item["price"]*1).toFixed(2);
					row.cells[3].innerHTML = (item["yield"]*1).toFixed(2) + "%";
				}
			});

			marketdata.loadCommodity(function(data){
				//缩短名称
				function shortName(name){
					return (name && name.length>5) ? name.substring(0, 5) : name;
				}
				// 在这里指定要显示的列表
				var names = { "布兰特原油":1, "纽约轻原油":1, "天然气期货":1, "燃油期货":1, "黄金期货":1, "铜期货":1, "BDI指数":1, "CRB指数":1, "高盛商品":1 };
				var trList = document.getElementById("yypricetable").getElementsByTagName("tr");
				var index = 1;
				for(var i=0; i<data.length; i++){
					if(index>=trList.length) break;
					if(names[data[i]["name"]]==1){
						var row = trList[index];
						row.cells[0].innerHTML = formatString("<span title='{0}'>{1}</span>", data[i]["name"], shortName(data[i]["name"]));
						row.cells[1].innerHTML = data[i]["price"].toFixed(3);
						row.cells[2].innerHTML = data[i]["percent"];
						row.cells[2].className = cssColor(data[i]["updown"]);
						index++;
					}
				}
			});
			//载入人民币牌价， bocArray为中国银行牌价，icbcArray为工商银行牌价
			marketdata.loadForexPrice(function(bocArray, icbcArray){
				//要显示的牌价名称
				var names = {"英镑":1,"港币":1,"美元":1,"瑞士法郎":1,"新加坡元":1,"日元":1,"加元":1,"欧元":1,"澳大利亚元":1,"澳门元":1,"新西兰元":1,"韩国元":1};
				var rows = document.getElementById("boc_forexprice").getElementsByTagName("tr");
				var index = 0;
				for(var i=0; i<bocArray.length && index<rows.length-1; i++){
					var item = bocArray[i];
					//列表里存在的名字才显示
					if(names[item["name"]]) {
						var row = rows[index+1];
						index++;
						row.cells[0].innerHTML = item["name"];
						row.cells[1].innerHTML = item["buyprice2"];
						row.cells[2].innerHTML = item["sellprice"];
					}
				}
			});
			//载入沪深涨跌成交额排行榜
			//回调参数callback(ranks["沪A涨幅"],ranks["沪A跌幅"],ranks["沪A成交额"],ranks["深A涨幅"],ranks["深A跌幅"],ranks["深A成交额"],ranks["中小板涨幅"],ranks["中小板跌幅"],ranks["中小板成交额"]);
			marketdata.loadQuotesRankOld(function(sha_up, sha_down, sha_volume, sza_up, sza_down, sza_volume, zx_up, zx_down, zx_volume){
				//将数据填充到表格,表格的行数支持最大为10行，最小1行
				function fillRank(tableId, rank, isVolume){
					var rows = document.getElementById(tableId).getElementsByTagName("tr");
					for(var i=0; i<rank.length && i<rows.length-1; i++){
						var row = rows[i+1];
						var item = rank[i];
						row.cells[0].innerHTML = formatString("<a href='http://quotes.money.163.com/{0}.html' target='_blank'>{1}</a>", item["code"], item["name"]);
						row.cells[1].innerHTML = item["price"];
						if(isVolume){//当前填充的是成交额榜
							row.cells[2].innerHTML = item["shareAmount"].toFixed(0);
						}else{
							row.cells[2].innerHTML = (item["updownRate"]*100).toFixed(2) + "%";
						}
						row.cells[2].className = cssColor(item["updownRate"]);//涨跌颜色
					}
				}
				//取到数据后填充：沪深涨幅榜，沪深跌幅榜，沪深成交额榜
				fillRank("rank_sha_up", sha_up);
				fillRank("rank_sza_up", sza_up);
				fillRank("rank_sha_down", sha_down);
				fillRank("rank_sza_down", sza_down);
				fillRank("rank_sha_volume", sha_volume, true);
				fillRank("rank_sza_volume", sza_volume, true);
			});
			//载入三市涨平跌信息
			marketdata.loadUpdownInfo(function(json){
				try{
				document.getElementById("updown_shaz").innerHTML = json["sha"]["shaz"];
				document.getElementById("updown_shap").innerHTML = json["sha"]["shap"];
				document.getElementById("updown_shad").innerHTML = json["sha"]["shad"];
				document.getElementById("updown_szaz").innerHTML = json["sza"]["szaz"];
				document.getElementById("updown_szap").innerHTML = json["sza"]["szap"];
				document.getElementById("updown_szad").innerHTML = json["sza"]["szad"];
				document.getElementById("updown_hs3z").innerHTML = json["hs3"]["hs3z"];
				document.getElementById("updown_hs3p").innerHTML = json["hs3"]["hs3p"];
				document.getElementById("updown_hs3d").innerHTML = json["hs3"]["hs3d"];
				}catch(ex){}
			});
			//加载行情实时数据
			ready(function(){
				jQuote.init({timeout:10000}).refresh(document.body).loadData();
			});
			//切换表单
			var market_tab = new NTES.ui.Slide(NTES("#market_tab > li"), NTES("#market > div"), "on", "mouseover"); // 财经行情图切换
			var newsrank_tab = new NTES.ui.Slide(NTES("#newsrank_tab > li"), NTES("#newsrank > div"), "on", "mouseover"); // 点击排行切换
			var zjfwg_tab = new NTES.ui.Slide(NTES("#zjfwg_tab > li"), NTES("#zjfwg > div"), "on", "mouseover"); // 最近访问股切换
			var zbxg_tab = new NTES.ui.Slide(NTES("#zbxg_tab > li"), NTES("#zbxg > div"), "on", "mouseover"); // 指标选股切换
			var zldx_tab = new NTES.ui.Slide(NTES("#zldx_tab > li"), NTES("#zldx > div"), "on", "mouseover"); // 主力动向切换
			var jdzdfb_tab = new NTES.ui.Slide(NTES("#jdzdfb_tab > li"), NTES("#jdzdfb > div"), "on", "mouseover"); // 阶段涨跌幅榜切换
			var zfb_tab = new NTES.ui.Slide(NTES("#zfb_tab > li"), NTES("#zfb > div"), "on", "mouseover"); // 涨幅榜切换
			var dfb_tab = new NTES.ui.Slide(NTES("#dfb_tab > li"), NTES("#dfb > div"), "on", "mouseover"); // 跌幅榜切换
			var cjeb_tab = new NTES.ui.Slide(NTES("#cjeb_tab > li"), NTES("#cjeb > div"), "on", "mouseover"); // 成交额榜切换
			var jjdata_tab = new NTES.ui.Slide(NTES("#jjdata_tab > li"), NTES("#jjdata > div"), "on", "mouseover"); // 基金数据切换
			var jjjz_tab = new NTES.ui.Slide(NTES("#jjjz_tab > li"), NTES("#jjjz > div"), "on", "mouseover"); // 基金净值切换
			var hkstockzdfb_tab = new NTES.ui.Slide(NTES("#hkstockzdfb_tab > li"), NTES("#hkstockzdfb > div"), "on", "mouseover"); // 港股涨跌幅榜切换
			var jrscdata_tab = new NTES.ui.Slide(NTES("#jrscdata_tab > li"), NTES("#jrscdata > div"), "on", "mouseover"); // 金融市场切换
			var pmbj_tab = new NTES.ui.Slide(NTES("#pmbj_tab > li"), NTES("#pmbj > div"), "on", "mouseover"); // 盘面报价切换
//]]>
</script>
